# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="fec58-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fec58-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fec58-104">L’élément **ResponseCode** fournit des informations sur l’état de la demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fec58-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="fec58-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fec58-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="fec58-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fec58-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="fec58-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fec58-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>
